-- Table structure for table `pmj_member_photo`

CREATE TABLE `pmj_member_photo` (
  `id` int(6) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `registration_id` int(12) NOT NULL,
  `filename` varchar(36) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `filename_thumb` varchar(36) NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('main','other') NOT NULL,
  `avatar` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `submit_date` datetime NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('pending','online','offline') CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=2937 ;
